Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ENTJ (Extraverted, Intuitive, Thinking, Judging), you are typically characterized by your assertiveness, strategic thinking, and strong leadership skills. You are highly organized and decisive, often taking charge of situations and making plans with precision. Your charisma and ability to inspire others make you a compelling leader, yet you can sometimes come across as domineering or overly competitive. You thrive on challenges and enjoy achieving goals through structured approaches, but this drive can sometimes lead to pushing others too hard or not allowing for enough flexibility. Your focus is often on the future and setting ambitious objectives, which can be both motivating and challenging for those around you.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 6
results: [6]

Your focus is often on the future and setting ambitious objectives, which can be both motivating and challenging for those around you.

Your enthusiasm for innovation and your ability to motivate others make you a compelling leader, yet you can sometimes come across as domineering or impatient with those who do not share your drive and efficiency. You prefer a structured environment and are highly organized, making you adept at managing multiple tasks simultaneously. Despite this, you may struggle with emotional depth and intimacy, valuing practicality and results over personal relationships.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: When someone thinks highly of you, you wonder how long it will take them to feel disappointed in you
response: 6
results: [5, 3, 3, 6, 5, 3, 5, 7, 6, 4, 2, 5, 6, 2, 6, 3, 5, 5, 6, 5, 2, 7, 5, 4, 4, 3, 2, 6, 6, 4, 3, 6, 3, 5, 6, 3, 7, 3, 5, 4, 3, 3, 4, 6, 3, 5, 2, 4, 2, 6]

Your extroverted nature makes you naturally outgoing and sociable, while your intuitive mind allows you to foresee possibilities and trends that others might overlook. Your thinking style prioritizes logic and reason, making you analytical and objective in decision-making, yet you can also be quite directive and prefer to lead. Your judging preference means you thrive on structure and organization, preferring to plan ahead and complete tasks systematically. This combination results in a dynamic and assertive personality who excels at problem-solving and driving projects forward.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You usually prefer just doing what you feel like at any given moment instead of planning a particular daily routine
response: 2
results: [3, 3, 5, 5, 4, 3, 5, 7, 6, 4, 3, 4, 6, 2]

Your intuitive tendency towards future possibilities can make you insightful and forward-thinking, yet it may sometimes lead to overthinking or planning too far ahead without considering all immediate realities. Your strong sense of purpose and determination can inspire those around you, but it might also come across as demanding or directive at times.

Your extroverted nature makes you highly sociable and communicative, yet you also possess a keen sense of judgment that allows you to make rational decisions based on data and facts. You are detail-oriented and efficient, capable of organizing tasks and environments to maximize productivity. However, you may sometimes struggle with showing empathy and can come across as somewhat cold or distant, as your focus tends to be on achieving results rather than nurturing personal relationships.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You are interested in so many things that you find it difficult to choose what to try next
response: 4
results: [4, 2, 3, 6, 2, 3, 5, 7, 5, 4, 4, 4, 6, 2, 4, 3, 5, 5, 4]

cycle: 7

Your decision-making process is swift and rational, guided by principles and objectives. You value efficiency and organization, and prefer to plan ahead to ensure everything runs smoothly. However, you might come across as somewhat impatient or dismissive of those who don't share your level of detail and structure.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You usually stay calm, even under a lot of pressure
response: 3
results: [4, 3, 3, 6, 3]

cycle: 9

You enjoy organizing and planning ahead, and you excel in environments that allow you to lead and influence others towards achieving common goals.
